**Tool Call: Read file `README.md`**
Status: Completed

```json
{
  "Text": "# spectralfilm-rs: Android Processing Engine\n\n> [!IMPORTANT]\n> At this stage, this project is very experimental and a work in progress. Things might change fast. This repository contains **only the headless processing engine**, rewritten in Rust and optimized for Android via JNI/NDK.\n\nAn exploration of how to make good use of spectroscopic data from manufacturer datasheets in an end-to-end, physically based model with spectral calculations, with the goal of turning that data into convincing film, print, and scan renderings natively on mobile devices.\n\nAn high-level writeup and discussion on the original desktop project is available on [discuss.pixls.us]().\n\nIn practice, `spectralfilm-rs` provides a high-performance computational photography backend. It lets you take linear RAW data directly from the Android camera sensor, pass it through a virtual negative, print, and scan pipeline, and calculate how film-stock data, couplers, grain, and halation shape the final result. The aim is not just to imitate a generic \"film look,\" but to build a model that stays connected to the structure and behavior of real photographic materials, all running within a strict mobile memory and performance budget.\n\n## Introduction\n\nThe simulation emulates negative or positive film emulsions starting from published data for film stocks. An example of the curves for Kodak Portra 400 (data-sheet e4050, 2016) is shown in the following figure (note that the CMY diffuse densities are generic because they are usually not published).\n\nAn example of data for Kodak Portra Endura print paper (data-sheet e4021, 2009) is shown in the next figure.\n\nThe left panel shows the spectral log sensitivities of each color layer. The central panel shows the log-exposure-density characteristic curves for each layer when the medium is exposed to a neutral gray gradient under a reference light. The panel on the right shows the absorption spectra of the dyes formed on the medium during chemical development.\n\nStarting from linear RGB data (ideally directly from a RAW buffer), the simulation reconstructs the spectral data, projects the virtual light transmitted through the negative onto print paper, and uses a simplified color enlarger with dichroic filters to balance the print.\n\nThe pipeline is sketched in this figure, adapted from [^1]:\n\n\nData-sheet curves are really not enough to reproduce a decent film look. The key is to understand that film emulsions contain couplers, chemicals that are produced during development alongside the actual CMY dyes, and these are very important for achieving the desired saturation. The main ones are:\n\n* **Masking couplers:** Give the typical orange color to unexposed developed film. These are simulated with a negative absorption contribution in the isolated dye absorption spectra.\n\n* **Direct inhibitor couplers:** Released locally when density is formed, inhibiting the formation of density in nearby layers. If we let the couplers diffuse in space, they increase local contrast and perceived sharpness.\n\n## Architecture & Layout\n\nSince this is the mobile processing port, all GUI elements have been stripped away in favor of a lean, native core. The codebase is organized into two primary crates:\n\n1. `spectralfilm-core`: Pure Rust runtime simulation pipeline. It handles the heavy lifting: spectral mathematics, stochastic grain generation, and dye absorption calculations. We are actively migrating complex spatial operations (like halation blurring) to Vulkan compute shaders to free up the CPU.\n2. `spectralfilm-ndk`: The JNI bridge exposing a C-ABI. This manages memory sharing between the JVM and Rust space, ensuring zero-copy buffer passing for large image arrays.\n\n## Installation & Building\n\nYou will need the Android NDK and Rust installed on your machine. We recommend using `cargo-ndk` for compilation.\n\n```bash\n# Install cargo-ndk\ncargo install cargo-ndk\n\n# Add Android targets\nrustup target add aarch64-linux-android armv7-linux-androideabi x86_64-linux-android\n\n# Clone the repository\ngit clone https://github.com/your-username/spectralfilm-rs.git\ncd spectralfilm-rs\n\n# Build the JNI libraries\ncargo ndk -t arm64-v8a -t x86_64 -o ./android/app/src/main/jniLibs build --release\n\n```\n\n## Android Usage\n\nThe core engine is designed to sit inside a RAW-first pipeline. For best results, intercept the image data from Camera2/CameraX before the ISP applies nonlinear tone mapping or noise reduction.\n\nMinimal Kotlin integration:\n\n```kotlin\nimport com.latentcam.spectralfilm.SpectralEngine\nimport com.latentcam.spectralfilm.SimulationParams\nimport com.latentcam.spectralfilm.profiles.KodakPortra400\nimport com.latentcam.spectralfilm.profiles.KodakPortraEndura\n\n// Initialize the native Rust engine\nval engine = SpectralEngine()\n\n// Configure the pipeline\nval params = SimulationParams.Builder()\n    .setFilmProfile(KodakPortra400())\n    .setPrintProfile(KodakPortraEndura())\n    .setHalation(size = 2.5f, strength = 0.15f)\n    .build()\n\n// Pass linear RAW data directly (e.g., from an ImageProxy or DngCreator buffer)\n// Engine processes via NDK and returns the developed byte array\nval processedBuffer = engine.processRaw(rawImageBuffer, width, height, params)\n\n// Clean up native resources\nengine.release()\n\n```\n\n## Testing\n\nTesting is handled via standard Rust tooling. Regression snapshots are stored as `.npz` files (parsed natively in tests) in `tests/baselines/`.\n\n```bash\ncargo test --release\n\n```\n\nWhen a simulation change is intentional and you need to update the mathematical baselines:\n\n```bash\ncargo run --bin regenerate_test_baselines\n\n```\n\n## Input Data & Performance Considerations\n\n* **Memory Management:** Processing 16-bit or 32-bit float buffers on mobile devices is memory intensive. Ensure your application requests `largeHeap=\"true\"` in the Android Manifest, and always manually release native buffers via the provided JNI hooks to prevent out-of-memory (OOM) crashes.\n* **Color Spaces:** The simulation expects linear, scene-referred data. Convert Android's sensor output into linear ProPhoto RGB or Rec2020 before passing the buffer to the Rust engine.\n\n## References\n\n[^1]: Giorgianni, Madden, Digital Color Management, 2nd edition, 2008 Wiley\n[^2]: Hung, The Reproduction of Color, 6th edition, 2004 Wiley\n[^3]: Mallett, Yuksel, Spectral Primary Decomposition for Rendering with sRGB Reflectance, Eurographics Symposium on Rendering - DL-only and Industry Track, 2019, doi:10.2312/SR.20191216"
}
```

**Tool Call: Read file `src\spektrafilm\runtime\params_schema.py`**
Status: Completed

```json
{
  "Text": "from __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\n\nfrom spektrafilm.profiles.io import Profile\n\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass DiffusionFilterParams:\n    active: bool = False\n    # filter_family selects PSF shape and absorption regime. Allowed values\n    # are the keys of `_DIFFUSION_FILTER_SHAPES` in spektrafilm.model.diffusion.\n    filter_family: str = \"black_pro_mist\"\n    # commercial filter stops: 0, 1/8, 1/4, 1/2, 1, 2 (interpolated in between)\n    strength: float = 0.5\n    # multiplier on image-plane PSF widths (all per-group lambdas)\n    spatial_scale: float = 1.0\n    # additive bias to the family's halo warmth axis. The halo is energy-\n    # conservingly redistributed across its sub-components per channel:\n    # warmth > 0 pushes warm light (R + slight G) toward the OUTER halo\n    # and cool light (B) toward the inner halo (and vice versa for\n    # warmth < 0). 0 = use family default. Effective warmth is soft-\n    # clamped to [-1.5, +1.5].\n    halo_warmth: float = 0.0\n    # Per-group fine-tune multipliers (advanced). Default 1.0 = use the\n    # family preset unchanged. `*_intensity` scales the corresponding\n    # group weight (w_c / w_h / w_b); the three weights are then\n    # renormalized so they still sum to 1, i.e. the kernel stays\n    # unit-normalised and the strength → p_s mapping is unchanged. So\n    # these knobs reshuffle the relative split of energy between core,\n    # halo and bloom, not the total deflected fraction. `*_size` scales\n    # each group's lambda_um uniformly (all sub-components in that group\n    # stretched by the same factor).\n    core_intensity: float = 1.0\n    core_size: float = 1.0\n    halo_intensity: float = 1.0\n    halo_size: float = 1.0\n    bloom_intensity: float = 1.0\n    bloom_size: float = 1.0\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass CameraParams:\n    exposure_compensation_ev: float = 0.0\n    auto_exposure: bool = True\n    auto_exposure_method: str = \"center_weighted\"\n    lens_blur_um: float = 0.0\n    film_format_mm: float = 35.0\n    filter_uv: tuple[float, float, float] = (0.0, 410.0, 8.0)\n    filter_ir: tuple[float, float, float] = (0.0, 675.0, 15.0)\n    diffusion_filter: DiffusionFilterParams = field(default_factory=DiffusionFilterParams)\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass EnlargerParams:\n    illuminant: str = \"TH-KG3\"\n    print_exposure: float = 1.0\n    print_exposure_compensation: bool = True\n    normalize_print_exposure: bool = True\n    y_filter_shift: float = 0.0\n    m_filter_shift: float = 0.0\n    y_filter_neutral: float = 55 # kodak cc values\n    m_filter_neutral: float = 65 # kodak cc values\n    c_filter_neutral: float = 0 # kodak cc values\n    lens_blur: float = 0.0\n    diffusion_filter: DiffusionFilterParams = field(default_factory=DiffusionFilterParams)\n    preflash_exposure: float = 0.0\n    preflash_y_filter_shift: float = 0.0\n    preflash_m_filter_shift: float = 0.0\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass ScannerParams:\n    lens_blur: float = 0.0\n    white_correction: bool = False\n    black_correction: bool = False\n    white_level: float = 0.98\n    black_level: float = 0.01\n    unsharp_mask: tuple[float, float] = (0.7, 0.7)\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass GrainParams:\n    active: bool = True\n    sublayers_active: bool = True\n    agx_particle_area_um2: float = 0.2\n    agx_particle_scale: tuple[float, float, float] = (0.8, 1.0, 2.0)\n    agx_particle_scale_layers: tuple[float, float, float] = (2.5, 1.0, 0.5)\n    density_min: tuple[float, float, float] = (0.07, 0.08, 0.12)\n    uniformity: tuple[float, float, float] = (0.97, 0.97, 0.99)\n    blur: float = 0.65\n    blur_dye_clouds_um: float = 1.0\n    micro_structure: tuple[float, float] = (0.2, 30)\n    n_sub_layers: int = 1\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass HalationParams:\n    active: bool = True\n    # high-level scalars (default 1.0 preserves the physical low-level defaults)\n    scatter_amount: float = 1.0\n    scatter_spatial_scale: float = 1.0\n    halation_amount: float = 1.0\n    halation_spatial_scale: float = 1.0\n    # in-emulsion scatter — energy-preserving mixture: Gaussian core + exponential\n    # tail (scatter_tail_um is the exponential decay constant, internally\n    # dispatched to a Gaussian mixture by fast_exponential_filter)\n    scatter_core_um: tuple[float, float, float] = (2.6, 2.3, 1.8)\n    scatter_tail_um: tuple[float, float, float] = (8.8, 7.0, 6.4)\n    scatter_tail_weight: tuple[float, float, float] = (0.74, 0.64, 0.64)\n    # highlight boost — reconstructs pre-clip irradiance before propagation\n    boost_ev: float = 0.0\n    boost_range: float = 0.3\n    protect_ev: float = 4.0\n    # back-reflection halation — additive sum of N Gaussians with sqrt(k) widths\n {
  "Text": "\"\"\"Runtime process entry points.\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom spektrafilm.runtime.params_schema import RuntimePhotoParams\nfrom spektrafilm.runtime.pipeline import SimulationPipeline\nfrom spektrafilm.utils.preview import resize_for_preview\nfrom spektrafilm.runtime.params_builder import (\n    digest_params,\n    init_params,\n)\n\nclass Simulator:\n    \"\"\"User-facing wrapper around the runtime simulation pipeline.\n    The params passed to the constructor should be static and not be changed.\n    They can be refreshed with update_params or soft_update, which delegate to the internal pipeline.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, params: RuntimePhotoParams):\n        self._pipeline = SimulationPipeline(params) # should stay private\n\n    def process(self, image):\n        \"\"\"Process the input image through the simulation pipeline and return the final result.\"\"\"\n        return self._pipeline.process(image)\n\n    def update_params(self, params):\n        \"\"\"Update the parameters of the simulation pipeline.\"\"\"\n        self._pipeline.update(params)\n\n    def soft_update(self, **kwargs):\n        \"\"\"Soft update parameters by only changing the provided fields, keeping the rest unchanged.\n        only selected safe parameters can be updated with this method\n        \"\"\"\n        self._pipeline.soft_update(**kwargs)\n\n    def get_timings(self):\n        \"\"\"Get the timings of the different stages of the simulation pipeline.\"\"\"\n        return self._pipeline.get_timings()\n\n    def get_total_elapsed_time(self):\n        \"\"\"Get the total wall-clock time of the last process call.\"\"\"\n        return self._pipeline.get_total_elapsed_time()\n\n    def format_timings(self):\n        \"\"\"Format the last recorded timings for display.\"\"\"\n        return self._pipeline.format_timings()\n\n    def print_timings(self):\n        \"\"\"Print the formatted timings of the last process call.\"\"\"\n        self._pipeline.print_timings()\n\n\n######################################################################################\n# Convenience functions for single-call simulation without needing to instantiate the Simulator class.\n\ndef simulate(image, params: RuntimePhotoParams,\n             digest_params_first: bool = True,\n             print_timings: bool = False):\n    \"\"\"Convenience function to run the simulation pipeline with a single call.\n    The simulator needs digested parameters to run. By default they are digested on the fly.\n    If you already have digested parameters or want to digest them yourself, set digest_params_first=False.\n    \"\"\"\n    if digest_params_first:\n        params = digest_params(params)\n    simulator = Simulator(params)\n    result = simulator.process(image)\n    if print_timings:\n        simulator.print_timings()\n    return result\n\n\ndef simulate_preview(image, params: RuntimePhotoParams,\n                     digest_params_first: bool = True,\n                     print_timings: bool = False):\n    \"\"\"Convenience function to run the simulation pipeline with a single call.\n    The simulator needs digested parameters to run. By default they are digested on the fly.\n    If you already have digested parameters or want to digest them yourself, set digest_params_first=False.\n    \"\"\"\n    max_size = params.settings.preview_max_size\n    result = simulate(resize_for_preview(image, max_size), params,\n                      digest_params_first=digest_params_first,\n                      print_timings=print_timings)\n    return result\n\n\n#######################################################################################################\n# Legacy for ART, to be removed in the future when the old API is fully deprecated.\n\nclass AgXPhoto(Simulator):\n    def __init__(self, params: RuntimePhotoParams):\n        digested_params = digest_params(params)\n        super().__init__(digested_params)\n\n# photo_params is init_params\ndef photo_params(film_profile, print_profile) -> RuntimePhotoParams:\n    \"\"\"Legacy helper to build a RuntimePhotoParams with default film and print profiles.\n    Build a runtime parameter object.\n    It needs to be digested with digest_params before being used in the runtime pipeline.\n    film_profile - label string for the film profile to use, e.g. \"kodak_portra_400\n    print_profile - label string for the print profile to use, e.g. \"kodak_portra_endura\"\n    \"\"\"\n    params = init_params(film_profile=film_profile, print_profile=print_profile)\n    params.io.full_image = True # legacy compatibility, has no effect\n    params.io.preview_resize_factor = 1.0 # legacy compatibility, has no effect\n    return params\n\n__all__ = [\n    \"RuntimePhotoParams\",\n    \"Simulator\",\n    \"simulate\",\n    \"simulate_preview\",\n    \"AgXPhoto\", # legacy for ART\n    \"photo_params\", # legacy for ART\n]"
}

  "Text": "from __future__ import annotations\n\nimport copy\nfrom time import perf_counter\n\nimport numpy as np\n\nfrom spektrafilm.runtime.services import (\n    EnlargerService,\n format_timings\n\n\n\nclass SimulationPipeline:\n    \"\"\"Thin runtime orchestrator that composes stage objects.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, params, update_params=False):\n        self._params = copy.deepcopy(params)\n\n        self.camera = self._params.camera\n        self.film = self._params.film\n        self.film_render = self._params.film_render\n        self.enlarger =       self.debug = self._params.debug\n        self.settings = self._params.settings\n\n        self.timings = {}\n        self._last_elapsed_time = None\n\n        self._resize_service = ResizingService(self.io, self.camera.film_format_mm)\n        if not update_params:\n            self._lut_service = SpectralLUTService(self.settings.lut_resolution)\n        self._enlarger_service = EnlargerService(self.enlarger)\n        self._color_reference_service = ColorReferenceService(self.film, self.film_render,\n                                                              self.print, self.print_render,\n                                                              self.scanner.black_correction, self.scanner.white_correction,\n                                                              self.scanner.black_level, self.scanner.white_level,\n                                                              self.io)\n\n        \n        self._filming_stage = FilmingStage(\n            self.film,\n            self.film_render,\n            self.camera,\n            self.io,\n            self.settings,\n            self._lut_service,\n            self._resize_service, # to get pixel size um for blurs\n            self._enlarger_service, # to compute and save density spectral midgray to balance print\n            self._color_reference_service,\n        )\n        self._printing_stage = PrintingStage(\n            self.film,\n            self.film_render,\n            self.print,\n            self.print_render,\n            self.enlarger,\n            self.settings,\n            self._lut_service,\n            self._enlarger_service,\n            self._resize_service, # to get pixel size um for diffusion filter\n            self._color_reference_service,\n        )\n        self._scanning_stage = ScanningStage(\n            self.film,\n            self.film_render,\n            self.print,\n  # timing communication\n        self._filming_stage.timings = self.timings\n        self._printing_stage.timings = self.timings\n        self._scanning_stage.timings = self.timings\n        self._lut_service.timings = self.timings\n\n    def process(self, image):\n        \"\"\"Process an image through the simulation pipeline.\"\"\"\n        self.timings.clear()\n        start = perf_counter()\n        try:\n            if self.debug.debug_mode == 'off':\n                image = self._pipeline(image)\n            else:\n                image = self._pipeline_debug(image)\n            return image\n        finally:\n            self._last_elapsed_time = perf_counter() - start\n\n    def get_timings(self):\n        return self.timings\n\n    def get_total_elapsed_time(self):\n        return self._last_elapsed_time\n\n    def format_timings(self):\n        return format_timings(\n            self.get_timings(),\n            total_elapsed_time=self.get_total_elapsed_time(),\n        )\n\n    def print_timings(self):\n        print(self.format_timings())\n    \n    def update(self, params):\n        \"\"\"Update params and re-initialize stages that depend on them.\"\"\"\n        self.__init__(params, update_params=True)\n        \n    def soft_update(self,\n                    exposure_compensation_ev=None,\n                    print_exposure=None,\n                    c_filter_neutral=None,\n                    m_filter_neutral=None,\n                    y_filter_neutral=None,\n                    film_density_curves=None,\n                    print_density_curves=None,):\n        invalidates_print_balance_reference = False\n        if exposure_compensation_ev is not None:\n            self.camera.exposure_compensation_ev = exposure_compensation_ev\n            invalidates_print_balance_reference = True\n        if print_exposure is not None:\n            self.enlarger.print_exposure = print_exposure\n        if c_filter_neutral is not None:\n            self.enlarger.c_filter_neutral = c_filter_neutral\n        if m_filter_neutral is not None:\n            self.enlarger.m_filter_neutral = m_filter_neutral\n        if y_filter_neutral is not None:\n            self.enlarger.y_filter_neutral = y_filter_neutral\n        if film_density_curves is not None:\n            self.film.data.density_curves = film_density_curves\n            invalidates_print_balance_reference = True\n        if print_density_curves is not None:\n            self.print.data.density_curves = print_density_curves\n        if invalidates_print_balance_reference:\n            (\n                self._enlarger_service.density_spectral_midgray,\n                self._enlarger_service.density_spectral_midgray_comp,\n            ) = self._filming_stage._compute_density_spectral_midgray_to_balance_print()\n        \n    # private methods\n    \n    def _pipeline(self, image):\n        image = self._preprocess(image)\n        if self.io.scan_film: # replace with route switch\n            rgb_scan = self._pipeline_scan_film(image)\n        else:\n            rgb_scan = self._pipeline_print(image)\n        return rgb_scan\n    \n    def _preprocess(self, image):\n        image = np.double(np.array(image)[:, :, 0:3])\n        image = self._filming_stage.auto_exposure(image) # autoexposure service?\n        image = self._resize_service.crop_and_rescale(image)\n        return image\n    \n    def _pipeline_scan_film(self, rgb_image):\n        log_raw_film = self._filming_stage.expose(rgb_image)\n        cmy_film = self._filming_stage.develop(log_raw_film)\n        rgb_scan = self._scanning_stage.scan(cmy_film)\n        return rgb_scan\n    \n    def _pipeline_print(self, rgb_image):\n        log_raw_film = self._filming_stage.expose(rgb_image)\n        cmy_film = self._filming_stage.develop(log_raw_film)\n        log_raw_print = self._printing_stage.expose(cmy_film)\n        cmy_print = self._printing_stage.develop(log_raw_print)\n        rgb_scan = self._scanning_stage.scan(cmy_print)\n        return rgb_scan\n    \n################################################################################\n    \n    # debug_methods\n\n    def _pipeline_debug(self, rgb_image):\n        if self.debug.debug_mode == \"output\":\n            return self._debug_output_pipeline(rgb_image)\n        elif self.debug.debug_mode == \"inject\":\n            return self._debug_inject_pipeline(rgb_image)\n    \n    def _debug_output_pipeline(self, rgb_image):\n        \"\"\"Run the pipeline with additional outputs for debugging.\"\"\"\n        rgb_image = self._preprocess(rgb_image)\n        log_raw_film = self._filming_stage.expose(rgb_image)\n        if self.debug.output_film_log_raw:\n            return log_raw_film\n        \n        cmy_film = self._filming_stage.develop(log_raw_film)\n        if self.debug.output_film_density_cmy:\n            return cmy_film\n        \n        log_raw_print = self._printing_stage.expose(cmy_film)\n        cmy_print = self._printing_stage.develop(log_raw_print)\n        if self.debug.output_print_density_cmy:\n            return cmy_print\n        \n        rgb_scan = self._scanning_stage.scan(cmy_print)\n        return rgb_scan\n    \n    def _debug_inject_pipeline(self, cmy_film):\n        \"\"\"Run the pipeline with additional inputs for debugging.\"\"\"\n        if self.debug.inject_film_density_cmy:\n            log_raw_print = self._printing_stage.expose(cmy_film)\n            cmy_print = self._printing_stage.develop(log_raw_print)\n            rgb_scan = self._scanning_stage.scan(cmy_print)\n            return rgb_scan\n\n"

(3.5, 2.2, 1.9)\n    return params\n\n\n# Halation low-level presets keyed by (use, antihalation). These set the\n# physical baselines from the private halation implementation notes §5-§6.1;\n# the user-facing knobs (scatter_amount, scatter_spatial_scale,\n# halation_amount, halation_spatial_scale) remain at 1.0 and let the user\n# push the effect stronger or weaker without editing the low-level\n# parameters.\n#\n# sigma_h is set by the base material:\n#   still -> triacetate, 120-140 um thick -> sigma_h ~= 65 um\n#   cine  -> PET,        95-125 um thick -> sigma_h ~= 50 um\n# halation_strength is set by the antihalation layer, from §5 ranges:\n#   strong -> Vision3, modern colour neg: a1^R ~ 0.005-0.02\n#   weak   -> older / mismatched AH:       a1^R ~ 0.02-0.08\n#   no     -> rem-jet removed / redscale:  a1^R ~ 0.08-0.25\n# Strength values below are a1 midpoints * 1/(1-rho) with rho=0.5 (~2x a1).\n_HALATION_PRESETS: dict[tuple[str, str], dict[str, tuple[float, float, float]]] = {\n    ('still', 'strong'): {'sigma_h': (65.0, 65.0, 65.0), 'strength': (0.015, 0.005, 0.0)},\n    ('still', 'weak'):   {'sigma_h': (65.0, 65.0, 65.0), 'strength': (0.08,  0.02,  0.0)},\n    ('still', 'no'):     {'sigma_h': (65.0, 65.0, 65.0), 'strength': (0.30,  0.10,  0.015)},\n    ('cine',  'strong'): {'sigma_h': (50.0, 50.0, 50.0), 'strength': (0.015, 0.005, 0.0)},\n    ('cine',  'weak'):   {'sigma_h': (50.0, 50.0, 50.0), 'strength': (0.08,  0.02,  0.0)},\n    ('cine',  'no'):     {'sigma_h': (50.0, 50.0, 50.0), 'strength': (0.30,  0.10,  0.015)},\n}\n\n\ndef _apply_halation_preset(params: RuntimePhotoParams) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Seed low-level halation parameters from the profile's use/antihalation tags.\"\"\"\n    if not params.film.is_film:\n        return\n    info = params.film.info\n    preset = _HALATION_PRESETS.get((info.use, info.antihalation))\n    if preset is None:\n        return\n    params.film_render.halation.halation_first_sigma_um = preset['sigma_h']\n    params.film_render.halation.halation_strength = preset['strength']\n\ndef _apply_print_specifics(params: RuntimePhotoParams) -> RuntimePhotoParams:\n    \"\"\"Apply print specific settings to the params.\"\"\"\n    # define here all the specifics to stocks that should be applied in params.print_render\n    return params\n\n\n__all__ = [\n    \"apply_database_neutral_print_filters\",\n    \"digest_params\",\n    \"init_params\",\n]\n"

       self._io.input_cctf_decoding,\n                method=self._camera.auto_exposure_method,\n            )\n            return image * 2 ** autoexposure_ev\n        return image\n\n kl->ijl\", light_preflash, sensitivity)\n            return raw_preflash * self._enlarger.preflash_exposure\n        return np.zeros((3,))\n\n    def _compute_exposure_factor_midgray(self, sensitivity, print_illuminant):\n        factor_midgray = _exposure_factor(sensitivity, print_illuminant, self._enlarger_service.density_spectral_midgray)\n        if self._enlarger.normalize_print_exposure:\n            return factor_midgray_comp / factor_midgray\n        elif self._enlarger.normalize_print_exposure and self._enlarger.print_exposure_compensation:\n            return factor_midgray_comp\n        elif self._enlarger.normalize_print_exposure and not self._enlarger.print_exposure_compensation:\n            return factor_midgray\n        else:\n            return 1.0\n\ndef _exposure_factor(sensitivity, print_illuminant, density_spectral_midgray):\n    light_midgray = geometric mean to normalize the exposure\n    raw_midgray_geomean = np.exp(np.mean(np.log(raw_midgray), axis=2, keepdims=True))\n    return 1 / raw_midgray_geomean"

  "Text": "from __future__ import annotations\n\nimport colour\nimport numpy as np\nfrom opt_einsum import contract\n\nfrom spektrafilm.config import STANDARD_OBSERVER_CMFS\nfrom        return self._apply_cctf_encoding_and_clip(rgb)\n\n    # private methods\n\n    def _density_to_rgb(self, density_channels: np.ndarray, *, use_lut: bool) -> np.ndarray:\n        if self._io.scan_film:\n            glare = None\n            density_min = -np.array(self._film_render.grain.density_min)\n            density_max = np.nanmax(self._film.data.density_curves, axis=0)\n            scan_illuminant = standard_illuminant(self._film.info.viewing_illuminant)\n        else:\n            glare = self._print_render.glare\n            density_min = np.nanmin(self._print.data.density_curves, axis=0)\n            density_max = np.nanmax(self._print.data.density_curves, axis=0)\n            scan_illuminant = standard_illuminant(self._print.info.viewing_illuminant)\n            \n        normalization = np.sum(scan_illuminant * STANDARD_OBSERVER_CMFS[:, 1], axis=0)\n\n        log_xyz = apply_cctf_decoding=False,\n                apply_cctf_encoding=True,\n            )\n        return np.clip(rgb, a_min=0, a_max=1)\n\n\n\n"

  "Text": "from typing import Literal, TypeAlias\n\nimport numpy as np\nfrom numpy.typing import NDArray\nfrom opt_einsum import contract\nfrom spektrafilm.model.couplers import apply_density_correction_dir_couplers\nfrom spektrafilm.model.density_curves import interpolate_exposure_to_density\nfrom spektrafilm.model.grain import apply_grain\nfrom spektrafilm.runtime.params_schema import DirCouplersParams, GrainParams\n\n\nFloatArray: TypeAlias = NDArray[np.float64]\nProfileType: TypeAlias = Literal['negative', 'positive']\n\n################################################################################\n# Emulsion helpers\n\ndef compute_density_spectral(\n    channel_density,\n    density_cmy,\n    base_density=None,\n):\n    density_spectral = contract('ijk, lk->ijl', density_cmy, np.asarray(channel_density))\n    if base_density is not None:\n        density_spectral += np.asarray(base_density)\n    return density_spectral\n\ndef develop_simple(\n    log_raw,\n    log_exposure,\n    density_curves,\n    gamma_factor=1.0,\n):\n    density_cmy = interpolate_exposure_to_density(log_raw, density_curves, log_exposure, gamma_factor)\n    return density_cmy\n\ndef develop(\n    log_raw: FloatArray,\n    pixel_size_um: float,\n    log_exposure: FloatArray,\n    density_curves: FloatArray,\n    density_curves_layers: FloatArray,\n    dir_couplers: DirCouplersParams,\n    grain: GrainParams,\n    profile_type: ProfileType,\n    gamma_factor: float = 1.0,\n    bypass_grain: bool = False,\n    use_fast_stats: bool = False,\n) -> FloatArray:\n    density_curves = np.asarray(density_curves)\n    normalized_density_curves = density_curves - {
  "Text": "import numpy as np\nimport scipy\nimport scipy.ndimage\nfrom spektrafilm.model.density_curves import interp_density_cmy_layers\nfrom spektrafilm.runtime.params_schema import GrainParams\nfrom spektrafilm.utils.fast_stats import fast_binomial, fast_poisson, fast_lognormal_from_mean_std\nfrom spektrafilm.utils.fast_gaussian_filter import fast_gaussian_filter\n\n################################################################################\n# Grain (very simple model)\n################################################################################\n\ndef layer_particle_model(density,\n                         density_max=2.2,\n                         n_particles_per_pixel=10,\n                         grain_uniformity=0.98,\n                         seed=None,\n                         blur_particle=0.0,\n                         method='poisson_binomial',\n                         use_fast_stats=False,\n                         ):\n    if seed is not None:\n        np.random.seed(seed) # scipy uses np.random\n    \n    probability_of_development = density/density_max\n    probability_of_development = np.clip(probability_of_development, 1e-6, 1-1e-6) # for safe calc\n    od_particle = density_max/n_particles_per_pixel\n    \n    grain = np.zeros_like(density)\n    if method=='gamma_beta':\n        gamma_rvs = scipy.stats.gamma.rvs\n        beta_rvs = scipy.stats.beta.rvs\n        seeds = gamma_rvs(n_particles_per_pixel/(1-grain_uniformity+1e-6), size=density.shape) * (1-grain_uniformity+1e-6)\n        grain = beta_rvs(probability_of_development*n_particles_per_pixel,\n                        (1-probability_of_development)*n_particles_per_pixel)*seeds*od_particle\n    elif method=='poisson_binomial':\n        if use_fast_stats:\n            binom_rvs = fast_binomial\n            poisson_rvs = fast_poisson\n        else:\n            binom_rvs = scipy.stats.binom.rvs\n            poisson_rvs = scipy.stats.poisson.rvs\n        saturation = 1 - probability_of_development*grain_uniformity*(1-1e-6)\n        seeds = poisson_rvs(n_particles_per_pixel/saturation)\n        grain = binom_rvs(seeds, probability_of_development)\n        grain = np.double(grain)*od_particle*saturation\n    \n    if blur_particle>0:\n        # grain = scipy.ndimage.gaussian_filter(grain, blur_particle*np.sqrt(od_particle))\n        grain = fast_gaussian_filter(grain, blur_particle*np.sqrt(od_particle))\n    return grain\n\ndef add_micro_structure(density_cmy_out, micro_structure, pixel_size_um):\n    grain_micro_structure_blur_pixel = micro_structure[0]/pixel_size_um\n    grain_micro_structure_sigma = micro_structure[1]*0.001/pixel_size_um  # grain microstructure[1] is in nm\n    if grain_micro_structure_sigma > 0.05:\n        clumping = fast_lognormal_from_mean_std(np.ones_like(density_cmy_out),\n                                                np.ones_like(density_cmy_out)*grain_micro_structure_sigma)\n        if grain_micro_structure_blur_pixel>0.4:\n            # clumping = scipy.ndimage.gaussian_filter(clumping, (grain_micro_structure_blur_pixel,\n            #                                                     grain_micro_structure_blur_pixel, 0))\n            clumping = fast_gaussian_filter(clumping, grain_micro_structure_blur_pixel)\n        density_cmy_out *= clumping\n    return density_cmy_out\n\ndef apply_grain_to_density(density_cmy,\n                           pixel_size_um=10,\n                           agx_particle_area_um2=0.2,\n                           agx_particle_scale=[1,0.8,3],\n                           density_min=[0.03,0.06,0.04],\n                           density_max_curves=[2.2,2.2,2.2],\n                           grain_uniformity=[0.98,0.98,0.98],\n                           grain_blur=1.0,\n                           n_sub_layers=1,\n                           fixed_seed=None,\n                           ):\n    density_min = np.array(density_min)\n    density_max = density_max_curves + density_min\n    pixel_area_um2 = pixel_size_um**2\n    agx_particle_area_um2 = agx_particle_area_um2*np.array(agx_particle_scale)\n    n_particles_per_pixel = pixel_area_um2/agx_particle_area_um2\n    sigma_blur_pixel = grain_blur\n    \n    if fixed_seed is not None:\n        seed = None\n    else:\n        seed = [0, 1, 2]\n    \n    if n_sub_layers>1:\n        n_particles_per_pixel /= n_sub_layers\n    \n    density_cmy += density_min\n    density_cmy_out = np.zeros_like(density_cmy)\n    for ch in np.arange(3):\n        for sl in np.arange(n_sub_layers):\n            density_cmy_out[:,:,ch] += layer_particle_model(density_cmy[:,:,ch],\n                                                            density_max=density_max[ch],\n                                                            n_particles_per_pixel=n_particles_per_pixel[ch],\n                                                            grain_uniformity=grain_uniformity[ch],\n                                                            seed=seed[ch] + sl*10)\n    density_cmy_out /= n_sub_layers\n    density_cmy_out -= density_min\n    \n    if sigma_blur_pixel>0.4:\n        # density_cmy_out = scipy.ndimage.gaussian_filter(density_cmy_out, (sigma_blur_pixel, sigma_blur_pixel, 0))\n        density_cmy_out = fast_gaussian_filter(density_cmy_out, sigma_blur_pixel)\n        \n    return density_cmy_out\n\n\n# experimental\ndef apply_grain_to_density_layers(density_cmy_layers, # x,y,sublayers,rgb\n                                  density_max_layers, # 3x3 [sublayers,rgb]\n                                  pixel_size_um=10,\n                                  agx_particle_area_um2=0.2,\n                                  agx_particle_scale=[1,0.8,3], # rgb\n                                  agx_particle_scale_layers=[3,1,0.3], # sublayers\n                                  density_min=[0.03,0.06,0.04],\n                                  grain_uniformity=[0.98,0.98,0.98],\n                                  grain_blur=1.0,\n                                  grain_blur_dye_clouds_um=1.0,\n                                  grain_micro_structure=(0.1, 30),\n                                  fixed_seed=None,\n                                  use_fast_stats=False,\n                                  ):\n    density_max_total = np.sum(density_max_layers, axis=0) # [sublayers,rgb]\n    density_max_fractions = density_max_layers/density_max_total[None,:]\n    density_min_layers = density_max_fractions*np.array(density_min)[None,:]\n    density_max_layers = density_max_layers + density_min_layers\n    \n    pixel_area_um2 = pixel_size_um**2\n    agx_particle_area_um2_layers = (agx_particle_area_um2 * \n                                    np.array(agx_particle_scale)[None,:] * \n                                    np.array(agx_particle_scale_layers)[:,None]) # layers, rgb\n    n_particles_per_pixel = pixel_area_um2*density_max_fractions/agx_particle_area_um2_layers\n\n    \n    if fixed_seed is not None:\n        seed = None\n    else:\n        seed = [0, 1, 2]\n    \n    density_cmy_layers += density_min_layers\n    density_cmy_out = np.zeros(density_cmy_layers.shape[0:3])\n    for ch in np.arange(3): # rgb channels\n        for sl in np.arange(3): # sublayers\n            density_cmy_out[:,:,ch] += layer_particle_model(density_cmy_layers[:,:,sl,ch],\n                                                            density_max=density_max_layers[sl,ch],\n                                                            n_particles_per_pixel=n_particles_per_pixel[sl,ch],\n                                                            grain_uniformity=grain_uniformity[ch],\n                                                            seed=seed[ch] + sl*10,\n                                                            blur_particle=grain_blur_dye_clouds_um,\n                                                            use_fast_stats=use_fast_stats)\n    \n    # micro-structure\n    density_cmy_out = add_micro_structure(density_cmy_out, grain_micro_structure, pixel_size_um)\n\n    # final\n    density_cmy_out -= density_min\n    if grain_blur>0:\n        # density_cmy_out = scipy.ndimage.gaussian_filter(density_cmy_out, (grain_blur, grain_blur, 0))\n        density_cmy_out = fast_gaussian_filter(density_cmy_out, grain_blur)\n    return density_cmy_out\n\n\ndef apply_grain(\n    density_cmy,\n    pixel_size_um,\n    grain: GrainParams,\n    density_curves,\n    density_curves_layers,\n    profile_type,\n    bypass_grain=False,\n    use_fast_stats=False,\n):\n    if not grain.active or bypass_grain:\n        return density_cmy\n\n    if not grain.sublayers_active:\n        density_max = np.nanmax(density_curves, axis=0)\n        return apply_grain_to_density(\n            density_cmy,\n            pixel_size_um=pixel_size_um,\n            agx_particle_area_um2=grain.agx_particle_area_um2,\n            agx_particle_scale=grain.agx_particle_scale,\n            density_min=grain.density_min,\n            density_max_curves=density_max,\n            grain_uniformity=grain.uniformity,\n            grain_blur=grain.blur,\n            n_sub_layers=grain.n_sub_layers,\n        )\n\n    density_cmy_layers = interp_density_cmy_layers(\n        density_cmy,\n        density_curves,\n        density_curves_layers,\n        positive_film=profile_type == 'positive',\n    )\n    density_max_layers = np.nanmax(density_curves_layers, axis=0)\n    return apply_grain_to_density_layers(\n        density_cmy_layers,\n        density_max_layers=density_max_layers,\n        pixel_size_um=pixel_size_um,\n        agx_particle_area_um2=grain.agx_particle_area_um2,\n        agx_particle_scale=grain.agx_particle_scale,\n        agx_particle_scale_layers=grain.agx_particle_scale_layers,\n        density_min=grain.density_min,\n        grain_uniformity=grain.uniformity,\n        grain_blur=grain.blur,\n        grain_blur_dye_clouds_um=grain.blur_dye_clouds_um,\n        grain_micro_structure=grain.micro_structure,\n        use_fast_stats=use_fast_stats,\n    )\n\n# TODO: make grain parameter with RMS granularity\n\nif __name__=='__main__':\n    density = np.ones((128,128))*2\n    g1 = layer_particle_model(density, density_max=2, n_particles_per_pixel=10, grain_uniformity=0.99, sigma_blur=0.)\n    g2 = layer_particle_model(density, density_max=2, n_particles_per_pixel=10, grain_uniformity=0.96, sigma_blur=0.)\n    print('g1 ------------------')\n    print('Density Test')\n    print('Mean', np.mean(g1))\n    print('RMS', np.std(g1)*1000)\n    print('Skewness', scipy.stats.skew(g1.flatten()))\n    print('Kurtosis', scipy.stats.kurtosis(g1.flatten()))\n    print('g2 ------------------')\n    print('Mean', np.mean(g2))\n    print('RMS', np.std(g2)*1000)\n    print('Skewness', scipy.stats.skew(g2.flatten()))\n    print('Kurtosis', scipy.stats.kurtosis(g2.flatten()))\n    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n    fig, axs = plt.subplots(1,2)\n    axs[0].imshow(g1, vmin=0, vmax=2.2)\n    axs[0].set_title('Uniformity=0.99')\n    axs[1].imshow(g2, vmin=0, vmax=2.2)\n    axs[1].set_title('Uniformity=0.96')\n    fig.suptitle('Fully saturated density with different uniformity')\n **Tool Call: Read file `src\spektrafilm\model\couplers.py`**

```json
{
  "Text": "import numpy as np\nfrom opt_einsum import contract\n\nfrom spektrafilm.runtime.params_schema import DirCouplersParams\nfrom spektrafilm.utils.fast_gaussian_filter import fast_gaussian_filter\nfrom spektrafilm.model.density_curves import interpolate_exposure_to_density\n\ndef compute_density_curves_before_dir_couplers(density_curves, log_exposure, dir_couplers_matrix, positive=False):\n    \"\"\"\n    DIR couplers affect the same layer by increasing contrast.\n    I suppose that in the design of a film this is taken into account, and the final film has well behaved density curves.\n    In order to get final curves for gray ramps equal to the input data, the density curves before the effect of the couplers are needed.\n\n    Args:\n        density_curves (numpy.array): Characteristic density curves of the film after the application of DIR couplers\n        log_exposure (numpy.array): The image as log_exposure\n        dir_couplers_matrix (_type_): DIR couplers matrix computed with compute_dir_couplers_matrix()\n\n    Returns:\n        numpy.array: Corrected density curves before the effect of DIR couplers\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    if positive:\n        # We are asusming that interimage effects in positve film are acting in the silver development stage\n        # We are also assuming that silver density is d_max - d\n        density_curves_silver = np.nanmax(density_curves, axis=0) - density_curves\n    else:\n        density_curves_silver = np.copy(density_curves)\n    \n    couplers_amount_curves = contract('jk, km->jm', density_curves_silver, dir_couplers_matrix)\n    log_exposure_0 = log_exposure[:,None] - couplers_amount_curves\n    density_curves_corrected = np.zeros_like(density_curves)\n    for i in np.arange(3):\n        if positive:\n            density_curves_corrected[:,i] = -np.interp(log_exposure, log_exposure_0[:,i], -density_curves[:,i])\n        else:\n            density_curves_corrected[:,i] = np.interp(log_exposure, log_exposure_0[:,i], density_curves[:,i])\n    return density_curves_corrected\n\n\ndef compute_dir_couplers_matrix(couplers_params: DirCouplersParams = DirCouplersParams()):\n    \"\"\"\n    Compute the inhibitors matrix using a simple diffusion model across layers.\n\n    Parameters:\n    amount_rgb (list of float): Amounts of dir couplers for RGB channels. Default is [0.7,0.7,0.5]. Typically 0-1 range.\n    layer_diffusion (float): Sigma for gaussian diffusion distance of dir couplers. Default is 1.\n\n    Returns:\n    numpy.ndarray: The computed inhibitors matrix.\n    Row index is the donor/source layer that releases inhibitor.\n    Column index is the receiving/affected layer whose exposure is reduced.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    M_self = np.array(couplers_params.gamma_samelayer_rgb)*couplers_params.inhibition_samelayer\n    M_self = np.diag(M_self)\n    M_inter = np.zeros((3,3))\n    # Off-diagonal terms follow the same convention: donor row, receiver column.\n    M_inter[0,1] = couplers_params.gamma_interlayer_r_to_gb[0]\n    M_inter[0,2] = couplers_params.gamma_interlayer_r_to_gb[1]\n    M_inter[1,0] = couplers_params.gamma_interlayer_g_to_rb[0]\n    M_inter[1,2] = couplers_params.gamma_interlayer_g_to_rb[1]\n    M_inter[2,0] = couplers_params.gamma_interlayer_b_to_rg[0]\n    M_inter[2,1] = couplers_params.gamma_interlayer_b_to_rg[1]\n    M_inter *= couplers_params.inhibition_interlayer\n    return M_self + M_inter\n\ndef compute_exposure_correction_dir_couplers(log_raw, density_cmy, density_max,\n                                             dir_couplers_matrix, diffusion_size_pixel,\n                                             high_exposure_couplers_shift=0.0,\n                                             positive=False):\n    \"\"\"\n    Apply coupler inhibitors to the raw data based on density curves and inhibitor values.\n    Coupler inhibitors are released when density is formed in the emulsion layers.\n    If a layer is dense, the inhibitors are released to prevent further density formation in neighboring layers.\n    Also self-inhibitors in the same layer, after spatial diffusion, can prevent further density formation\n    in nearby areas, adding a local contrast effect.\n\n    Parameters:\n    raw (numpy.ndarray): The raw data to which inhibitors will be applied.\n    density_cmy (numpy.ndarray): The density values for each layer.\n    density_max (float): The maximum density value achievable for each layer, used for normalization.\n    dir_couplers_matrix (numpy.ndarray): The inhibitors matrix. Fisrt index is the input layer, second index is the output layer.\n    diffusion_size_pixel (int): The size of the gaussian filter for the diffusion of the inhibitors in xy.\n    high_exposure_couplers_shift (float): if overexposure increases saturation, this will increase the inhibitors effect at higher density\n    \n    Returns:\n    numpy.ndarray: The modified raw exposure data after applying the effect of inhibitors.\n    \"\"\"\n    if positive:\n        density_silver = density_max - density_cmy\n    else:\n        density_silver = np.copy(density_cmy)\n    density_silver += high_exposure_couplers_shift*density_silver**2\n    # density_silver[..., k] generated in donor layer k contributes to receiver m\n    # through dir_couplers_matrix[k, m].\n    log_raw_correction = contract('ijk, km->ijm', density_silver, dir_couplers_matrix)\n    if diffusion_size_pixel>0:\n        # log_raw_correction = gaussian_filter(log_raw_correction, (diffusion_size_pixel, diffusion_size_pixel, 0))\n        log_raw_correction = fast_gaussian_filter(log_raw_correction, diffusion_size_pixel)\n    log_raw_corrected = log_raw - log_raw_correction\n    return log_raw_corrected\n\n\ndef apply_density_correction_dir_couplers(\n    density_cmy,\n    log_raw,\n    pixel_size_um,\n    log_exposure,\n    density_curves,\n    dir_couplers,\n    profile_type,\n    gamma_factor=1.0,\n):\n    if not dir_couplers.active:\n        return density_cmy\n\n    positive = profile_type == 'positive'\n    \n    couplers_matrix = compute_dir_couplers_matrix(dir_couplers)\n    couplers_matrix *= dir_couplers.amount\n    \n    density_curves_0 = compute_density_curves_before_dir_couplers(\n        density_curves,\n        log_exposure,\n        couplers_matrix,\n        positive=positive,\n    )\n    density_max = np.nanmax(density_curves, axis=0)\n    diffusion_size_pixel = dir_couplers.diffusion_size_um / pixel_size_um\n    log_raw_0 = compute_exposure_correction_dir_couplers(\n        log_raw,\n        density_cmy,\n        density_max,\n        couplers_matrix,\n        diffusion_size_pixel,\n        positive=positive,\n    )\n    return interpolate_exposure_to_density(log_raw_0, density_curves_0, log_exposure, gamma_factor)\n\nif __name__=='__main__':\n    # # Test the raw correction coupler inhibitors\n    # log_raw = np.ones((4,4,3))\n    # density_cmy = np.ones((4,4,3))\n    # density_max = 2.2\n    # couplers_amount = [0.9,0.7,0.5]\n    # diffusion_size_pixel = 2\n    # log_raw = raw_correction_dir_couplers(log_raw, density_cmy, density_max, couplers_amount, diffusion_size_pixel)\n    # print(log_raw)\n\n    couplers_params = DirCouplersParams()\n    M = compute_dir_couplers_matrix(couplers_params)\n    print(M)"

{
  "Text": "from __future__ import annotations\n\nimport numpy as np\nfrom typing import Callable\nfrom colour import RGB_to_RGB\n\nfrom spektrafilm.model.emulsion import develop_simple\n\nclass ColorReferenceService:\n    \"\"\"Manages the color reference for black and white corrections.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, film_profile,  film_render,\n                       print_profile, print_render,\n                       black_correction, white_correction,\n                       black_level, white_level,\n                       io_params):\n        self._film = film_profile\n        self._film_render = film_render\n        self._print = print_profile\n        self._print_render = print_render\n        self._scan_film = io_params.scan_film\n        self._output_color_space = io_params.output_color_space\n        self._output_cctf_encoding = io_params.output_cctf_encoding\n\n        self._black_correction = black_correction\n        self._white_correction = white_correction\n        self._black_level = _remove_sRGB_cctf(black_level)\n        self._white_level = _remove_sRGB_cctf(white_level)\n        \n        # local memory for black and white reference densities, to avoid redundant calculations during correction\n        self._y_black = None # positive film or print cmy density for black\n        self._y_white = None # positive film or print cmy density for white\n        self._black_white_exposure_correction = None # exposure correction factor to apply to the print exposure based on the black and white reference densities\n        \n        # communication with the scanning stage\n        self.cmy_to_log_xyz = None # callable to convert cmy densities to log xyz, to be defined in the scanning stage during pipeline init!\n        self.log_raw_print_black = None\n        self.log_raw_print_white = None\n\n    # public methods\n\n    def _update_cmy_black_white_references(self, in_print=False):\n        if not self._black_correction and not self._white_correction:\n            return\n        elif self._scan_film and self._film.info.type == 'negative':\n            return\n        else:\n            if self._scan_film and self._film.info.type == 'positive' and not in_print:\n                cmy_black = np.nanmax(self._film.data.density_curves, axis=0)[None, None, :]\n                cmy_white = np.zeros((1, 1, 3))\n                log_xyz_black = self.cmy_to_log_xyz(cmy_black)\n                log_xyz_white = self.cmy_to_log_xyz(cmy_white)\n                self._y_black = (10 ** log_xyz_black)[:, :, 1]\n                self._y_white = (10 ** log_xyz_white)[:, :, 1]\n            elif not self._scan_film and self._print.info.type == 'negative' and in_print:\n                cmy_black = develop_simple(\n                    self.log_raw_print_black,\n                    self._print.data.log_exposure,\n                    self._print.data.density_curves,\n                    gamma_factor=self._print_render.density_curve_gamma,\n                )\n                cmy_white = develop_simple(\n                    self.log_raw_print_white,\n                    self._print.data.log_exposure,\n                    self._print.data.density_curves,\n                    gamma_factor=self._print_render.density_curve_gamma,\n                )\n                log_xyz_black = self.cmy_to_log_xyz(cmy_black)\n                log_xyz_white = self.cmy_to_log_xyz(cmy_white)\n                self._y_black = (10 ** log_xyz_black)[:, :, 1]\n                self._y_white = (10 ** log_xyz_white)[:, :, 1]\n            return\n    \n    def black_white_filming_exposure_correction(self): # in filming and printing\n        if not self._black_correction and not self._white_correction:\n            return 1.0\n        elif self._film.info.type == 'negative':\n            return 1.0\n        elif self._scan_film and self._film.info.type == 'positive':\n            density_midgray = -np.log10(0.184)\n            self._update_cmy_black_white_references(in_print=False)\n            midgray_corrected = self._correction_fucntion()[1]\n            density_midgray_corrected = -np.log10(midgray_corrected)\n            density_curve_av = np.nanmean(self._film.data.density_curves, axis=1)\n            density_min_av = np.nanmean(self._film.data.base_density)\n            log_exposure = self._film.data.log_exposure\n            log_exposure_midgray_corrected = -np.interp(-(density_midgray_corrected-density_min_av), \n                                                -density_curve_av, log_exposure)\n            log_exposure_midgray = -np.interp(-(density_midgray-density_min_av),\n                                                -density_curve_av, log_exposure)\n            exposure_correction = 10 ** (log_exposure_midgray_corrected - log_exposure_midgray)\n            return 1/exposure_correction\n        else:\n            return 1.0\n\n    def black_white_printing_exposure_correction(self): # in printing\n        if not self._black_correction and not self._white_correction:\n            return 1.0\n        elif self._print.info.type == 'negative':\n            density_midgray = -np.log10(0.184)\n            self._update_cmy_black_white_references(in_print=True)\n            midgray_corrected = self._correction_fucntion()[1]\n            density_midgray_corrected = -np.log10(midgray_corrected)\n            density_curve_av = np.nanmean(self._print.data.density_curves, axis=1)\n            density_min_av = np.nanmean(self._print.data.base_density)\n            log_exposure = self._print.data.log_exposure\n            log_exposure_midgray_corrected = np.interp(density_midgray_corrected-density_min_av, \n                                                density_curve_av, log_exposure)\n            log_exposure_midgray = np.interp(density_midgray-density_min_av,\n                                                density_curve_av, log_exposure)\n            exposure_correction = 10 ** (log_exposure_midgray_corrected - log_exposure_midgray)\n            return exposure_correction\n\n    def black_white_xyz_correction(self, xyz): # in scanning\n        \"\"\"Apply black and white correction to the XYZ values,\n        based on the black and white reference densities\n        cmy_to_log_xyz() must be defined in the scanning stage and passed to convert cmy densities\n        \"\"\"\n        if not self._black_correction and not self._white_correction:\n            return xyz\n        if self._scan_film and self._film.info.type == 'negative':\n            return xyz # do not correct negative film scans\n        else:\n            correction_func, _ = self._correction_fucntion()\n            y = xyz[:, :, 1]\n            y_corrected = correction_func(y)\n            scale = y_corrected / (y + 1e-10)\n            return xyz * scale[:, :, None]\n\n\n    def _correction_fucntion(self):\n        white_level = self._white_level\n        black_level = self._black_level\n        if self._black_correction and not self._white_correction:\n            white_level = self._y_white\n        if self._white_correction and not self._black_correction:\n            black_level = self._y_black\n        if self._black_correction or self._white_correction:                           \n            m = (white_level - black_level) / (self._y_white - self._y_black + 1e-10)\n            q = black_level - m * self._y_black\n            def correction_func(y):\n                return np.clip(m * y + q, 0, 1)\n        midgray_black_white_corrected = (0.184 - q)/m\n        return correction_func, midgray_black_white_corrected\n\n# private functions\n    \ndef _remove_sRGB_cctf(y_input):\n    return RGB_to_RGB(y_input*np.ones((1,1,3)),\n                    'sRGB',\n                    'sRGB',\n                    apply_cctf_decoding=True,\n                    apply_cctf_encoding=False,\n                ).mean()\n    \n"
}

**Tool Call: Read file `src\spektrafilm\utils\spectral_upsampling.py`**

```json
{
  "Text": "import numpy as np\nimport struct\nimport colour\nimport scipy\nimport importlib.resources\nfrom opt_einsum import contract\nimport scipy.interpolate\n\nfrom spektrafilm.utils.fast_interp_lut import apply_lut_cubic_2d\nfrom spektrafilm.config import SPECTRAL_SHAPE, STANDARD_OBSERVER_CMFS\nfrom spektrafilm.model.illuminants import standard_illuminant\n\n################################################################################\n# LUT generatation of irradiance spectra for any xy chromaticity\n# Thanks to hanatos for providing luts and sample code to develop this. I am grateful.\n\ndef _load_coeffs_lut(filename='hanatos_irradiance_xy_coeffs_250304.lut'):\n    # load lut of coefficients for efficient computations of irradiance spectra\n    # formatting\n    header_fmt = '=4i'\n    header_len = struct.calcsize(header_fmt)\n    pixel_fmt = '=4f'\n    pixel_len = struct.calcsize(pixel_fmt)\n\n    package = importlib.resources.files('spektrafilm.data.luts.spectral_upsampling')\n    resource = package / filename\n    with resource.open(\"rb\") as file:\n        header = file.read(header_len)\n        _, _, width, height = struct.Struct(header_fmt).unpack_from(header)\n        px = [[0] * height for _ in range(width)]\n        for j in range(height):\n            for i in range(width):\n                data = file.read(pixel_len)\n                px[i][j] = struct.Struct(pixel_fmt).unpack_from(data)\n    return np.array(px)\n\ndef _tri2quad(tc):\n    # converts triangular coordinates into square coordinates.\n    # for better sampling of the visible locus of xy chromaticities.\n    # the lut is represented in triangular coordinates\n    tc = np.array(tc)\n    tx = tc[...,0]\n    ty = tc[...,1]\n    y = ty / np.fmax(1.0 - tx, 1e-10)\n    x = (1.0 - tx)*(1.0 - tx)\n    x = np.clip(x, 0, 1)\n    y = np.clip(y, 0, 1)\n    return np.stack((x,y), axis=-1)\n\ndef _quad2tri(xy):\n    # converts square coordinates into triangular coordinates\n    x = xy[...,0]\n    y = xy[...,1]\n    tx = 1 - np.sqrt(x)\n    ty = y * np.sqrt(x)\n    return np.stack((tx,ty), axis=-1)\n\ndef _fetch_coeffs(tc, lut_coeffs):\n    # find the coefficients for spectral upsampling of given rgb coordinates\n    # if color_space!='ITU-R BT.2020' or apply_cctf_decoding:\n    #     rgb = colour.RGB_to_RGB(rgb, input_colourspace=color_space, apply_cctf_decoding=apply_cctf_decoding,\n    #                                     output_colourspace='ITU-R BT.2020', apply_cctf_encoding=False)\n    #     rgb = np.clip(rgb,0,1)\n    # xyz = colour.RGB_to_XYZ(rgb, colourspace='ITU-R BT.2020', apply_cctf_decoding=False)\n    # b = np.sum(xyz, axis=-1)\n    # xy = xyz[...,0:2] / b[...,None]\n    # tc = _tri2quad(xy)\n    coeffs = np.zeros(np.concatenate((tc.shape[:-1],[4])))\n    x = np.linspace(0,1,lut_coeffs.shape[0])\n    for i in np.arange(4):\n        coeffs[...,i] = scipy.interpolate.RegularGridInterpolator((x,x), lut_coeffs[:,:,i], method='cubic')(tc)\n    return coeffs\n\ndef _compute_spectra_from_coeffs(coeffs, smooth_steps=1):\n    wl = SPECTRAL_SHAPE.wavelengths\n    wl_up = np.linspace(360,800,441) # upsampled wl for finer initial calculation 0.5 nm\n    x = (coeffs[...,0,None] * wl_up + coeffs[...,1,None])*  wl_up  + coeffs[...,2,None]\n    y = 1.0 / np.sqrt(x * x + 1.0)\n    spectra = 0.5 * x * y +  0.5\n    spectra /= coeffs[...,3][...,None]\n    \n    # gaussian smooth with smooth_step*sigmas and downsample\n    step = np.mean(np.diff(wl))\n    spectra = scipy.ndimage.gaussian_filter(spectra, step*smooth_steps, axes=-1)\n    def interp_slice(a, wl, wl_up):\n        return np.interp(wl, wl_up, a)\n    spectra = np.apply_along_axis(interp_slice, axis=-1, wl=wl, wl_up=wl_up, arr=spectra)\n    return spectra\n\ndef compute_lut_spectra(lut_size=128, smooth_steps=1, lut_coeffs_filename='hanatos_irradiance_xy_coeffs_250304.lut'):\n    v = np.linspace(0,1,lut_size)\n    tx,ty = np.meshgrid(v,v, indexing='ij')\n    tc = np.stack((tx,ty), axis=-1)\n    lut_coeffs = _load_coeffs_lut(lut_coeffs_filename)\n    coeffs = _fetch_coeffs(tc, lut_coeffs)\n    lut_spectra = _compute_spectra_from_coeffs(coeffs, smooth_steps=smooth_steps)\n    lut_spectra = np.array(lut_spectra, dtype=np.half)\n    return lut_spectra\n\ndef _load_hanatos2025_spectra_lut(filename='irradiance_xy_tc.npy'):\n    data_path = importlib.resources.files('spektrafilm.data.luts.spectral_upsampling').joinpath(filename)\n    with data_path.open('rb') as file:\n        spectra_lut = np.double(np.load(file))\n    return spectra_lut\n\ndef _illuminant_to_xy(illuminant_label):\n    illu = standard_illuminant(illuminant_label)\n    xyz = np.zeros((3))\n    for i in np.arange(3):\n        xyz[i] = np.sum(illu * STANDARD_OBSERVER_CMFS[:][:,i])\n    xy = xyz[0:2] / np.sum(xyz)\n    return xy\n\ndef _rgb_to_tc_b(rgb, color_space='ITU-R BT.2020', apply_cctf_decoding=False, reference_illuminant='D55'):\n    # source_cs = colour.RGB_COLOURSPACES[color_space]\n    # target_cs = source_cs.copy()\n    # target_cs.whitepoint = ILLUMINANTS['CIE 1931 2 Degree Standard Observer']['D65']\n    # adapted_rgb = colour.RGB_to_RGB(rgb, input_colourspace=source_cs,\n    #                                 output_colourspace=target_cs,\n    #                                 adaptation_transform='Bradford')    \n    # illu_xy = colour.CCS_ILLUMINANTS['CIE 1931 2 Degree Standard Observer'][reference_illuminant]\n    illu_xy = _illuminant_to_xy(reference_illuminant)\n    xyz = colour.RGB_to_XYZ(rgb, colourspace=color_space,\n                            apply_cctf_decoding=apply_cctf_decoding,\n                            illuminant=illu_xy,\n                            chromatic_adaptation_transform='CAT02')\n    b = np.sum(xyz, axis=-1)\n    xy = xyz[...,0:2] / np.fmax(b[...,None], 1e-10)\n    xy = np.clip(xy,0,1)\n    tc = _tri2quad(xy)\n    b = np.nan_to_num(b)\n    return tc, b\n\n################################################################################\n# From [Mallett2019]\n\nMALLETT2019_BASIS = colour.recovery.MSDS_BASIS_FUNCTIONS_sRGB_MALLETT2019.copy().align(SPECTRAL_SHAPE)\ndef rgb_to_raw_mallett2019(RGB, sensitivity,\n                           color_space='sRGB', apply_cctf_decoding=True,\n                           reference_illuminant='D65'):\n    \"\"\"\n    Converts an RGB color to a raw sensor response using the method described in Mallett et al. (2019).\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    RGB : array_like\n        RGB color values.\n    illuminant : array_like\n        Illuminant spectral distribution.\n    sensitivity : array_like\n        Camera sensor spectral sensitivities.\n    color_space : str, optional\n        The color space of the input RGB values. Default is 'sRGB'.\n    apply_cctf_decoding : bool, optional\n        Whether to apply the color component transfer function (CCTF) decoding. Default is True.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    raw : ndarray\n        Raw sensor response.\n    \"\"\"\n    illuminant = standard_illuminant(reference_illuminant)[:]\n    basis_set_with_illuminant = np.array(MALLETT2019_BASIS[:])*np.array(illuminant)[:, None]\n    lrgb = colour.RGB_to_RGB(RGB, color_space, 'sRGB',\n                    apply_cctf_decoding=apply_cctf_decoding,\n                    apply_cctf_encoding=False)\n    lrgb = np.clip(lrgb, 0, None)\n    raw  = contract('ijk,lk,lm->ijm', lrgb, basis_set_with_illuminant, sensitivity)\n    raw = np.nan_to_num(raw)\n    raw = np.ascontiguousarray(raw)\n    \n    raw_midgray  = np.einsum('k,km->m', illuminant*0.184, sensitivity) # use 0.184 as midgray reference\n    return raw / raw_midgray[1] # normalize with green channel\n\n################################################################################\n# Using hanatos irradiance spectra generation\n\nHANATOS2025_SPECTRA_LUT = _load_hanatos2025_spectra_lut()\n\ndef compute_hanatos2025_tc_lut(sensitivity, spectra_lut=HANATOS2025_SPECTRA_LUT):\n    raw_lut = contract('ijl,lm->ijm', spectra_lut, sensitivity)\n    return raw_lut\n\ndef rgb_to_raw_hanatos2025(rgb, sensitivity,\n                           color_space, apply_cctf_decoding, reference_illuminant, tc_lut=None):\n    tc_raw, b = _rgb_to_tc_b(\n        rgb,\n        color_space=color_space,\n        apply_cctf_decoding=apply_cctf_decoding,\n        reference_illuminant=reference_illuminant,\n    )\n    if tc_lut is None:\n        tc_lut  = compute_hanatos2025_tc_lut(sensitivity)\n    raw = apply_lut_cubic_2d(tc_lut, tc_raw)\n    raw *= b[...,None] # scale the raw back with the scale factor\n    # note that sensitivities are already normalized in balancing such that raw_midgray is 1, so no need to normalize here\n    return raw\n\ndef rgb_to_smooth_spectrum(rgb, color_space, apply_cctf_decoding, reference_illuminant):\n    # direct interpolation of the spectra lut, to be used only for smooth spectra close to white\n    tc_w, b_w = _rgb_to_tc_b(\n        rgb,\n        color_space=color_space,\n        apply_cctf_decoding=apply_cctf_decoding,\n        reference_illuminant=reference_illuminant,\n    )\n    v = np.linspace(0, 1, HANATOS2025_SPECTRA_LUT.shape[0])\n    spectrum_w = scipy.interpolate.RegularGridInterpolator((v,v), HANATOS2025_SPECTRA_LUT)(tc_w)\n    spectrum_w *= b_w\n    return spectrum_w.flatten()\n\n\nif __name__=='__main__':\n    lut_coeffs = _load_coeffs_lut()\n    coeffs = _fetch_coeffs(np.array([[1,1]]) ,lut_coeffs)\n    spectra = _compute_spectra_from_coeffs(coeffs)\n    lut_spectra = compute_lut_spectra(lut_size=128)\n"
}

  "Text": "import numpy as np\nimport scipy\nfrom spektrafilm.utils.fast_interp import fast_interp\n\n################################################################################\n# Denstity curves\n################################################################################\n\ndef interpolate_exposure_to_density(log_exposure_rgb, density_curves, log_exposure, gamma_factor):\n    \"\"\"\n    Interpolates the exposure values to density values using the provided density curves.\n    Parameters:\n    log_exposure_rgb (numpy.ndarray): A 3D array of shape (height, width, 3) representing the log10 RGB exposure values.\n    density_curves (numpy.ndarray): A 2D array of shape (num_points, 3) representing the density curves for each channel.\n    log_exposure (numpy.ndarray): A 1D array of logarithmic exposure values.\n    gamma_factor (float): The gamma correction factor to be applied to the density characteristic curves.\n    Returns:\n    numpy.ndarray: A 3D array of shape (height, width, 3) representing the interpolated density values in CMY channels.\n    \"\"\"\n    if np.size(gamma_factor)==1:\n        gamma_factor = [gamma_factor, gamma_factor, gamma_factor]\n    gamma_factor = np.array(gamma_factor)\n    density_cmy = np.zeros((log_exposure_rgb.shape[0], log_exposure_rgb.shape[1], 3))\n    # Shape (n,3).\n    factor (float, optional): The factor by which to reduce the light exposure values of the shadows. (brighter shadows). Default is 0.1.\n    density (float, optional): The density value of the transition point. Default is 1.2.\n    transition (float, optional): The transition density range used for Gaussian filtering. Default is 0.3.\n    Returns:\n    numpy.ndarray: density curves with viewing glare compensation removed.\n    \"\"\"\n    def _measure_slope(le, density_curve, le_center, range_ev=1):\n        le_delta = np.log10(2**range_ev)/2\n        le_0 = le_center - le_delta\n        le_1 = le_center + le_delta\n        density_0 = np.interp(le_0, le, density_curve)\n        density_1 = np.interp(le_1, le, density_curve)\n        slope = (density_1 - density_0)/(le_1 - le_0)\n        return slope    \n    \n    dc_mean = np.mean(dc, axis=1)\n    le_center = np.interp(density, dc_mean, le)\n    slope = _measure_slope(le, dc_mean, le_center)\n    le_step = np.mean(np.diff(le))\n    dc_out = np.zeros_like(dc)\n    for i in np.arange(3):\n        le_nl = np.copy(le)\n        le_nl[le>le_center] -= (le[le>le_center]-le_center)*factor\n        le_transition = transition/slope\n        le_nl = scipy.ndimage.gaussian_filter(le_nl, le_transition/le_step)\n        dc_out[:,i] = np.interp(le_nl, le, dc[:,i])\n    return dc_out"
}

  "Text": "import numpy as np\nimport scipy\nimport colour\nimport scipy.interpolate\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nfrom spektrafilm.config import SPECTRAL_SHAPE\nfrom spektrafilm.utils.io import load_dichroic_filters, load_filter\n\n################################################################################\n# Color Filter class\n################################################################################\n\ndef create_combined_dichroic_filter(wavelength,\n                                    transitions,\n                                    edges,\n                                    ):\n    # data from https://qd-europe.com/se/en/product/dichroic-filters-and-sets/\n    dichroics = np.zeros((np.size(wavelength),3))\n    dichroics[:,2] = scipy.special.erf( (wavelength-edges[0])/transitions[0])\n    dichroics[:,1][wavelength<=550] = -scipy.special.erf( (wavelength[wavelength<=550]-edges[1])/transitions[1])\n    dichroics[:,1][wavelength>550] = scipy.special.erf( (wavelength[wavelength>550]-edges[2])/transitions[2])\n    dichroics[:,0] = -scipy.special.erf( (wavelength-edges[3])/transitions[3])\n    dichroics = dichroics/2 + 0.5\n    return dichroics\n\nclass DichroicFilters():\n    def __init__(self,\n                 brand='thorlabs'):\n        self.wavelengths = SPECTRAL_SHAPE.wavelengths\n        self.filters = np.zeros((np.size(self.wavelengths), 3))\n        if brand == 'custom':\n            self.create_custom_filters()\n        else:\n            self.filters = load_dichroic_filters(self.wavelengths, brand)\n            \n    def plot(self):\n        colors = ['tab:cyan', 'tab:pink', total_filter = np.prod(dimmed_filters, axis=1)\n        filtered_illuminant = illuminant*total_filter\n        return filtered_illuminant\n    \n    def apply_cc(self, illuminant,             edges=[516,500,610,607],\n                               transitions=[12,8,8,8]):\n        self.filters = create_combined_dichroic_filter(self.wavelengths,\n                                                       transitions=transitions,\n                                                       edges=edges)\n\nclass GenericFilter():\n    def __init__(self,\n                 name='KG3',\n value=1.0):\n        dimmed_filter = 1 - (1-self.transmittance)*value\n        filtered_illuminant = illuminant*dimmed_filter\n        return filtered_illuminant\n\n################################################################################\n# Band pass filter\n\ndef sigmoid_erf(x, center, width=1):\n    return scipy.special.erf((x-center)/width)*0.5+0.5\n\ndef compute_band_pass_filter(filter_uv=[1, 410, 8], filter_ir=[1, 675, 15]):\n    amp_uv = filter_uv[0]\n    wl_uv = filter_uv[1]\n    width_uv = filter_uv[2]\n    \n    amp_ir = filter_ir[0]\n    wl_ir = filter_ir[1]\n    width_ir = filter_ir[2]\n    \n    amp_uv = np.clip(amp_uv, 0, 1)\n    amp_ir = np.clip(amp_ir, 0, 1)\n    \n    wl = SPECTRAL_SHAPE.wavelengths\n    filter_uv  = 1-amp_uv + amp_uv*sigmoid_erf(wl, wl_uv, width=width_uv)\n    filter_ir  = 1-amp_ir + amp_ir*sigmoid_erf(wl, wl_ir, width=-width_ir)\n    band_pass_filter = filter_uv * filter_ir\n    return  band_pass_filter\n        \n\n# color filter variables\ndichroic_filters = DichroicFilters()\nthorlabs_dichroic_filters =   "Text": "import numpy as np\nfrom scipy.ndimage import gaussian_filter\n\nfrom spektrafilm.utils.fast_stats import fast_lognormal_from_mean_std\nfrom spektrafilm.utils.fast_gaussian_filter import fast_gaussian_filter\n\n\ndef add_glare(xyz: np.ndarray, illuminant_xyz: np.ndarray, glare) -> np.ndarray:\n    if glare is not None and glare.active and glare.percent > 0:\n        glare_amount = compute_random_glare_amount(\n            glare.percent,\n            glare.roughness,\n            glare.blur,\n            xyz.shape[:2],\n        )\n        xyz = xyz + glare_amount[:, :, None] * illuminant_xyz[None, None, :]\n    return xyz\n\ndef compute_random_glare_amount(amount, roughness, blur, shape):\n    random_glare = fast_lognormal_from_mean_std(amount*np.ones(shape),\n                                                roughness*amount*np.ones(shape))\n    # random_glare = gaussian_filter(random_glare, blur)\n    random_glare = fast_gaussian_filter(random_glare, blur)\n    random_glare /= 100\n    return random_glare"
